  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_860372904" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/860372904" />
    <a title="Nereyda (Nick &amp; Nereyda&#39;s Infinite Booklist)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5383215-nereyda-nick-nereyda-s-infinite-booklist"><img alt="Nereyda (Nick &amp; Nereyda&#39;s Infinite Booklist)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1445582024p2/5383215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/860372904?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nereyda (Nick &amp; Nereyda&#39;s Infinite Booklist)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nereyda (Nick &amp; Nereyda&#39;s Infinite Booklist)" href="/user/show/5383215-nereyda-nick-nereyda-s-infinite-booklist">Nereyda (Nick &amp; Nereyda&#39;s Infinite Booklist)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer860372904&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer860372904" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16999691644252364448"><b>1.5/5 stars</b><br/><br/>I think, or at least I hope, that by know you guys know me well enough to know that I'm not the type of reader that loves to hate on hyped books. If I love or hate a book, I don't care how hyped or popular the book or author is, you will get my honest opinion no matter what. I will be the first to admit that I am a huge fan of Colleen Hoover's writing. Her books are always high on my favorites lists and she is an auto-read author for me. Despite the fact that I did not like this book </span>
  <span id="freeText16999691644252364448" style="display:none"><b>1.5/5 stars</b><br><br>I think, or at least I hope, that by know you guys know me well enough to know that I'm not the type of reader that loves to hate on hyped books. If I love or hate a book, I don't care how hyped or popular the book or author is, you will get my honest opinion no matter what. I will be the first to admit that I am a huge fan of Colleen Hoover's writing. Her books are always high on my favorites lists and she is an auto-read author for me. Despite the fact that I did not like this book at all and that it didn't work for me one bit, she is still one of my favorite authors and I will still be rushing to read her next book. Unfortunately, and it pains me to have to say this, but November 9 just wasn't for me.<br><br>From the summary, this book always made me a little nervous for several reasons. 1) It immediately reminded me of the plot for One Day. 2) I always have issues with romances that start from just one day of knowing each other. 3) The hint about Ben possibly hiding something had me worried this would have one of those shock value plot twists, which I normally hate. But, it's Colleen-freaking-Hoover and there was no way I was not reading this book. I was super excited to get an early copy and despite the fact that October was only reserved for Netflix binging, I couldn't help myself and had to read this book. The thing that upsets me the most is that November 9 had so much potential and the first few chapters showed so much promise. At first, it was just a few things here and there that bothered me, but eventually almost everything started bothering me and combined, it just didn't make this an enjoyable book for me. Since there were so many things that bothered me, I'm gonna list these in a non-spoiler and spoiler section below. If you are avoiding spoilers, simply skip that part and head to the end to my non-spoilery final thoughts. :)<br><br><b>Non-spoiler list of things that bothered me:</b><br>- The first thing I had an issue with was the fact that Fallon was scarred on most of her body and face from a house fire that cost her her acting career. Now, I'm not this monster that expects or wants all MC's to be perfect and beautiful and flawless, but this goes back to one of my main problems that I have with New Adult and the fact that everything has to be so fucking tragic. I thought we were at the point in NA where we were past characters needing a tragic past, but apparently not.<br><br>-Speaking of New Adult, my friend Megan wrote an awesome <a href="http://readingbookslikeaboss.com/dear-new-adult-an-almost-breakup-letter/" rel="nofollow noopener">Almost Break-Up Letter to New Adult</a> last week and while I was reading it and was agreeing with all her points, I would have never thought a Hoover book would fall victim to so many of those annoying and cliché NA traits. We had tragic pasts for both characters, drama overkill, plot twists that felt like they were simply added for the sake of shock value, recycled tropes that have already been done in previous/popular NA books, super cheesy lines, and conflict that seemed really forced. Just to name a few.<br><br>- Ben was too perfect in an unrealistic way. Hoover's male characters always seem to have this really intense feel to them, which I don't mind at all. But in Ben's case, there always felt something off about him. He literally came out of nowhere to save the day and offer to be Fallon's pretend boyfriend in front of her dad. What would have resulted in a one time thing turned into so much more when he stayed with her a few hours while she packed for New York and broke down barriers that no one else could in only a few hours, like letting him take off her clothes. He said just the right things to make Fallon feel better about her scars. He asked Fallon to date around while she was in New York for a year so she didn't 'miss anything', and he sounded like an inspirational coach half the time while the other half he said some really cheesy shit. Things like:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"Baby," he says, his lips forming a smile. "You already made this the best sex I've had , and I'm not even inside you yet."</i>
</blockquote><br>and this lovely gem as he's about to take her virginity:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"Fallon," he whispers, dragging his lips slowly across mine. "Thank you for this beautiful gift."</i>
</blockquote><br>-And speaking of cheese, Fallon said some really cheesy stuff too that made me roll my eyes.<br><blockquote>
  <i>It felt as if the second we joined together, a tiny piece of our souls got confused and a piece of his fell into me and a piece of mine fell into him.</i>
</blockquote><br>or:<br><blockquote>
  <i>I just know that there is no way I can tell him goodbye after this. It'll tear me apart, way worse than last year. I can't go another day without him being a part of my everyday life. Not after this.</i>
</blockquote><br>Keep in mind that this is after he 3rd November 9th they have spent together, roughly 12 hours they have spent together in total since they first met and after the first time they have sex....<br><br>- Towards the end of the book, by about the fifth November 9th they've spent together, Ben and Fallon have only spent a grand total of 28 hours together. This is one of the main reasons why I had such a hard time connecting with not only the story, but with Ben and Fallon as a couple. As stated in the summary, Fallon and Ben only meet once a year on November 9th, the day they met. This all sounds romantic, but it didn't work for me in a number of ways. Ben and Fallon agree for some reason (more on that later) that they should have zero contact at all during the years they are apart. They block each other on social media, they never give each other their phone numbers or emails so they don't talk, text or email. Basically, they just show up to an agreed location on November 9th at a certain time and hope the other is there. They have no idea if either of them have met someone else or any of the normal every day things that happen in life. Meanwhile, they always act like theirs is an epic love story despite the fact that in reality they just really basically strangers who happen to have a 'connection.' Each time they met, we had 1-2 chapters in his point-of-view and in her point-of-view and it was on to the next year.<br><br>-The fact that this was sort of a book with in a book felt like a cheap ploy to quickly address and dismiss any issues the reader may have, which honestly felt like an insult to us readers. Because Fallon is an avid reader (and gets Ben to read books too) and Ben is a writer, they kind of make fun of certain book scenarios while falling victim to those clichés. Fallon tells Ben early on that she hates insta-love and when she explains to him what insta-love is and he says that it sounds like what they must have, she quickly dismisses it. Years later when it comes up again, we are supposed to buy this half-assed explanation with this:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"You know how much I dislike insta-love."<br>"Oh, it was still insta-love," I tell her. "But ours is legit."</i>
</blockquote><br>Isn't that what every author says about their insta-love romance in books? Later on when they have sex, Ben muses about how as an author he has no words to describe that moment in paper so he will just have to... fade to black. Which is exactly what the book does at that moment. After reading Ugly Love, we all know Hoover is capable of writing really great and classy sex scenes. This approach came off as lazy. It felt like Hoover used the fact that Ben was an author, and Fallon was a reader to shut down any problems. I mentioned earlier that the plot of this book reminded me of One Day by David Nichols (which I have read). There is a scene in here that really bothered me when someone brings up the comparison:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"It's a little bit like Sleepless In Seattle'" Tate says.<br>I immediately shake my head. "It's nothing like that. They only agreed to meet once."<br>"True. I's like One Day, then. That movie with Anne Hathaway?"<br>Again, I dismiss her comparison. "That just focuses on one particular day every year, but the two people still interact throughout the year like normal. Fallon and I have no contact."<br>I don't know why I'm being so defensive. I think writers just naturally become defensive when their ideas are compared to other ideas, even if it's done innocently. But mine and Fallon's story is one-of-a-kind, and I feel somewhat protective of it.</i>
</blockquote><br>I don't like the fact that an international best seller book is reduced to simply an 'Anne Hathaway' movie. I especially dislike it since Hoover is an author herself. I'm sure it was innocent, but this bothered me.<br><br>-Another one of my issues with this story is that the conflict always felt forced. The reason why Fallon moves to New York is because he mother says that you don't know who you are until you are 23 years old, and you shouldn't date until then because if you don't know yourself how can you fall in love. And she always listens to her mother because her mother is always right. Something that Fallon feels the need to remind us of several times. So, she moves to New York to try to find herself and put herself out there to try to help out her career. This is all fine, but Fallon is 18 and alone and miserable in New York. And this doesn't explain the fact that she and Ben can't talk on the damn phone or text or email each other, even as friends. Years later, when Ben wants to move to New York to be with Fallon so they could be together, a family tragedy forces Ben to stay home. Or should I say, convinces Fallon that Ben has to stay home and once again can't have any contact with her. For his own good, of course. All of this just felt really forced to me.<br><br><b>Spoiler things that bothered me:</b><br>-When Fallon breaks Ben's heart and leaves to New York again, she shows up the next November 9th expecting to find a happy-go-lucky Ben. Instead, Ben is dating his dead brother's ex-wife and is raising his brother's son with her. She is hurt and angry, even though she's the one that told him to stay to help her. Even though she's the one that left without refusing to give him her number. She says something that really annoys me:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"And no matter who is at fault for that, whether it's mine for walking away last year or yours for not knowing I did it for your own good, none of it changes things."</i>
</blockquote><br>The whole 'I did it for your own good' move is stupid and condescending and overdone.<br><br>- Plot twist: It turns out that Ben is the one that set fire to Fallon's dad's house two years ago. Intentionally. That day he pretended to be her boyfriend, he was following her dad and fully knew who she was. This kind of negated all the 'your scars are what makes you beautiful' and 'you are lucky to be alive' and all that other after-school speeches he gave her. After that, I never really knew if he really felt that way, or if it was out of guilt for being the cause of that. I know this came as a huge shock to most readers, but it only annoyed me because the whole 'I'm responsible for your traumatic accident and now I'm gonna seek you out to ease my guilt' has been done before in Ten Tiny Breaths by KA Tucker and Leaving Paradise by Simone Elkeles.<br><br>- The reason that Ben set Fallon's dad's house on fire is because Ben's mom killed herself. He found some letters with his name on them and he assumed that they had an affair and he was responsible for his mom killing herself. I would also like to point out that this assumption is incorrect.<br><br>- Not only did Fallon have a tragic past (the fire), but Ben did too (his mom killing herself). This felt like overkill for a number of reasons. Ben's mother had terminal cancer and she didn't want to be a burden on her sons. So she shot herself in the head. In their home. Knowing that Ben was there at the time and he would be the one to find her since it was only the two of them that lived there. How terrible and fucked up is that reasoning? Couldn't have she taken pills or something that wouldn't result with her brains being splattered all over her bedroom? What was worse was the suicide note she left for him:<br><blockquote>
  <i>I know this will be difficult for you to deal with, so I've tried to make it as easy as possible. Someone will need to clean up after they take my body, so I've left a card on the kitchen counter for who you should call. There's plenty of cash in my purse. I've left it in the kitchen, on the counter.'</i>
</blockquote><br>Someone give her the mother of the year award so being so thoughtful!<br><br>- In case you missed it, Ben's mom killed herself on November 9. That same day he sets he fire that ruined Fallon's life. Two years later, that's the day they first officially meet. So that date has an important significance for a number of reasons. All of which I'm sure were meant to add to this supposedly epic romance, but only ended up being over he top.<br><br><b>Spoiler-free final thoughts:</b><br>I'm not saying that you should not read this book or that's its terrible, because a) that's a shitty thing to say and b) everyone has different tastes. Just because I thought this was Hoover's weakest book and I pretty much hated it, there is no denying that she is one hell of a talented writer. I just honestly think that this was missing the certain.... Hoover feel that makes all her other books stand out and hit you right in the feels. The fact that every single review on Goodreads is 5 stars and nothing less, really makes me question the state of book blogging right now and how honest certain people can be when it comes to reviewing hyped books or books by author 'friends'... I also really wish authors would find beta readers that aren't friends that can be truly objective...<br><br>November 9 was one of my most anticipated books of the year and I don't know if I'm more disappointed in the fact that this didn't work for me because it's written by Colleen Hoover, or of the fact that this Colleen Hoover book didn't work for me. If you're on the fence about this, I suggest you read reviews by bloggers you truly trust. And if you do decide to read this book, I hope you like it better than I did. No matter what I thought about this book, I'll always be looking forward to read her upcoming books and I still consider her one of my favorites.<br><br><a href="http://i1064.photobucket.com/albums/u367/nereyda1003/Blog%20Design%20Items/NickNereydaHeader_zpsxfz5gnpw.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445582039i/16677203._SX540_.png" width="300' alt=" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_860433999" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/860433999" />
    <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs"><img alt="Amy | Foxy Blogs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366176904p2/9955253.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/860433999?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amy | Foxy Blogs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amy | Foxy Blogs" href="/user/show/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs">Amy | Foxy Blogs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Amy | Foxy Blogs by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/1609377-kara">Kara</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=5-star-2015">5-star-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=arc-or-netgalley">arc-or-netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=2015-books">2015-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9955253-amy-foxy-blogs?shelf=october-2015">october-2015</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer860433999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1292525272780538416">Two words -<b> absolutely brilliant! </b><br/><br/>I’m amazed at CoHo's ability to deliver a unique story with each and every one of her books. After I was done with <b>November 9</b> I spent a good hour or two discussing it with Kara. There’s so much I want to say about it but really you can only do that with people who have read the book so not to ruin the story for others.<br/><br/>One thing that surprised me was when a certain couple made a cameo. It put a smile on my face. I'm so use to CoHo not following book trends that i</span>
  <span id="freeText1292525272780538416" style="display:none">Two words -<b> absolutely brilliant! </b><br><br>I’m amazed at CoHo's ability to deliver a unique story with each and every one of her books. After I was done with <b>November 9</b> I spent a good hour or two discussing it with Kara. There’s so much I want to say about it but really you can only do that with people who have read the book so not to ruin the story for others.<br><br>One thing that surprised me was when a certain couple made a cameo. It put a smile on my face. I'm so use to CoHo not following book trends that it was pleasant surprise to see the crossover. <br><br>CoHo’s men have a way of getting me worked up and not in a good way. It started with her first book Slammed and has continued on in her other books. While they make me want to smash my kindle against a wall, they also make me appreciate the realness of the situation. CoHo's love stories are guaranteed to have the ability to provoke strong emotions in the reader.<br><br>My favorite aspect of the story is how the book flowed so well together even though the story took place over a large time span. The story didn’t have any mundane lulls filled with everyday stuff. It held me captive from the opening scene until the very end. <br><br><b>I LOVED IT!!</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389785076ra/8054288.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>P.S. I love that CoHo commented on my status update. It made my year. <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user_status/show/78212009">https://www.goodreads.com/user_status...</a><br><br>✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦✦<br><b>RELEASE DATE:November 10, 2015 </b><br>Pre-order | order: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1ZGkYCP">http://amzn.to/1ZGkYCP</a><br><br><b>STANDALONE</b><br><br>**Complimentary copy in exchange for an honest review.**<br><br><a href="http://foxyblogs.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1442610494i/16258382._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_2092592767" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2092592767" />
    <a title="Ashwood (애쉬 우드)." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50173624-ashwood"><img alt="Ashwood (애쉬 우드)." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596432515p2/50173624.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2092592767?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ashwood (애쉬 우드)." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ashwood (애쉬 우드)." href="/user/show/50173624-ashwood">Ashwood (애쉬 우드).</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2092592767" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12957765624622922203">"One of the things I always try remind myself is that everyone has scars. A lot of them even worse than mine. The only difference is that mine are visible and most people's aren't."<br/><br/>I loved this book from page one. The writing style, characters, and story plot completely had me hooked. <br/><br/>November 9 tore out my heart, put it back together again, and majorly messed with my emotions.To say this was an emotional roller coaster is an understatement. <br/><br/>Fallon and Ben were perfect, scarred, and healing toge</span>
  <span id="freeText12957765624622922203" style="display:none">"One of the things I always try remind myself is that everyone has scars. A lot of them even worse than mine. The only difference is that mine are visible and most people's aren't."<br /><br />I loved this book from page one. The writing style, characters, and story plot completely had me hooked. <br /><br />November 9 tore out my heart, put it back together again, and majorly messed with my emotions.To say this was an emotional roller coaster is an understatement. <br /><br />Fallon and Ben were perfect, scarred, and healing together but perfect. Since the moment they met they were the fresh air in each other's life. They unconsciously made the other feel like they could be best they could be, they were honest to a fault, and as much as I don't really care for Insta love stories.. this one stole my heart. They had their struggles, fears, hopes, dreams but they were each others supporter in every aspect. Even if they only met once a year, for five years. <br /><br />Everyone makes mistakes and sometimes the consequences stay with you your whole life and plague you with guilt, like it did for Ben. But then one day, what you expect to be the worst thing ever turns out to be exactly opposite and your world aligns itself and puts your priorities in order, that's what happened to Ben. <br /><br />Fallon, having gone through a traumatic incident 2 years ago, meets someone outta the blue on one of the worst anniversaries of the year and that changes everything. <br /><br />The middle and almost end ripped out my heart and left it in tatters... I cried way more than I'd like to admit. The ending however, righted everything. This book was amazing. <br /><br />And finally one of my favorite quotes has got to be this one: <br /><br />"Yes, you have scars. But anyone who sees your scars before they see you doesn't deserve you. I hope you remember that and believe that. A body is simply a package for the true gifts inside. And you are full of gifts. Selflessness, kindness, compassion. All the things that matter. <br /> Youth and beauty fade. Human decency doesn't."<br /> -Ben</span>
  <a data-text-id="12957765624622922203" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_866275337" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/866275337" />
    <a title="ily " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22496761-ily"><img alt="ily " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599357419p2/22496761.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/866275337?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ily " class="user" itemprop="url" name="ily " href="/user/show/22496761-ily">ily </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22496761-ily?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22496761-ily?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22496761-ily?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer866275337" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18156859016474603021">Ugh, I hate NA. Basically CoHo books are the only ones I can stand in the sea of clichés that is this genre. But after <i>Confess</i> and this new novel I seriously think I should stay away from New Adult books forever.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>And somehow, with the way he’s looking down at me, I even believe I’m beautiful.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448489322i/17149194.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>@ NA AUTHORS please STOP with the bullshit of the girl with low self-esteem and the guy who's hidding a secret. STOP writing insecure girls who fall for the douchey <i>"you don't know you're beautifu</i></span>
  <span id="freeText18156859016474603021" style="display:none">Ugh, I hate NA. Basically CoHo books are the only ones I can stand in the sea of clichés that is this genre. But after <i>Confess</i> and this new novel I seriously think I should stay away from New Adult books forever.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>And somehow, with the way he’s looking down at me, I even believe I’m beautiful.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448489322i/17149194.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>@ NA AUTHORS please STOP with the bullshit of the girl with low self-esteem and the guy who's hidding a secret. STOP writing insecure girls who fall for the douchey <i>"you don't know you're beautiful, that's what makes you beautiful"</i> boyfriend. STOP writing relationships that are based on LIES and SECRETS. STOP writing slut-shaming bff's. Please....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448490679i/17149325.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On page five I was excited. On page fifty I had a terrible feeling about this read. One page 100 I wanted to cry because every single thing these characters said was cheesy and dumb. Honestly, guys, IT WAS SO BASIC AND SO WRONG. I would've never expected this from CoHo. Just look at these quotes:<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>I laugh again, and then I press my face to his chest and hug him back, <b>because why couldn’t he have been there the second I woke up in the hospital two years ago? Why did I have to go two whole years before finally being given the tiniest bit of confidence?</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448491680i/17149458.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You wear your hair like you do because you don’t want people to see too much of you. You wear long sleeves and collared shirts because you think it helps. But it doesn’t.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448492160i/17149489.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's definitely a fan of One Direction. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“<b>I don’t want to be your first, Fallon. I want to be your last.</b>”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448492160i/17149490.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sorry I just threw up in my mouth a little bit.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“<b>Baby,</b>” he says, his lips forming a smile. “<b>You have already made this the best sex I’ve ever had, and I’m not even inside you yet.</b>”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448493149i/17149590.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oops, it happened again. <br><br>Not only are Ben and Fallon walking clichés but the plot-twist is something you would find in -you guessed right!- any other book of the genre. But I wonder if it can really be considered a plot-twist since it couldn't have been more obvious. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“<b>Does she know, Ben? Does she have any idea that you’re the one who started that fire? That you’re the reason she almost died?</b>”</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448495237i/17149937._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nice try but it was too obvious, honey.<br><br>So Ben lied about everything and instead of telling her the truth about the accident first-hand, he made her fall in love with him and wrote a book about their beautiful story blah blah blah. So yeah, it gets worse: <br><br><i>
  <blockquote>I make a new pile with the pages I’ve already read. I stare down at the manuscript in disbelief. <b>I know I should be angry that he’s lied to me for so long, but being in his head is somehow justifying his behavior to me. And not only that, but it’s also justifying my father ’s behavior.</b>
</blockquote>
</i><br><br>You know that's what abusers do, right?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448495373i/17149958.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>We were drawn to each other. We made each other happy. And I know without a doubt there were several times during the past few years that we were madly in love with each other at the same time. Not everyone experiences that Fallon, and I’d be lying if I said I regretted it.</i>
</blockquote><br><br>SO YOU DON'T REGRET CAUSING THE ACCIDENT THAT ALMOST CLAIMED HER LIFE, TELLING EVERYTHING ABOUT IT TO YOUR BROTHER SO YOU COULD BOTH PROMISED YOU WON'T TELL IT WAS YOUR FAULT?????????????<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448491680i/17149458.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>I should have given you the chance to explain it then. If I had just listened to you, then we could have avoided an entire year of heartache. So for that.... I’m sorry. I’m so sorry. And I hope you can forgive me.”</i>
</blockquote><br><br>BYE.<br>I AM DONE.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1448494109i/17149737.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_860340718" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/860340718" />
    <a title="Vilma Iris" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15777655-vilma-iris"><img alt="Vilma Iris" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501855386p2/15777655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/860340718?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vilma Iris" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vilma Iris" href="/user/show/15777655-vilma-iris">Vilma Iris</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer860340718" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11730315223837435501"><b>The perfect blend of sexiness, emotion and intrigue. It's Colleen's best, most exciting book to date.</b><br/><br/>Colleen Hoover’s one-of-a-kind style of storytelling shines with November 9—a story about a boy and a girl who fall in love, one day at a time. But it’s also so much more. It’s lines of words that tell the story of a girl scarred by an event that made her feel less, made her feel abandoned. A girl whose dreams vanquished with the flames that ravaged her. It’s about a boy, a writer—Benton Kessler—</span>
  <span id="freeText11730315223837435501" style="display:none"><b>The perfect blend of sexiness, emotion and intrigue. It's Colleen's best, most exciting book to date.</b><br /><br />Colleen Hoover’s one-of-a-kind style of storytelling shines with November 9—a story about a boy and a girl who fall in love, one day at a time. But it’s also so much more. It’s lines of words that tell the story of a girl scarred by an event that made her feel less, made her feel abandoned. A girl whose dreams vanquished with the flames that ravaged her. It’s about a boy, a writer—Benton Kessler—who searches for inspiration and finds it the day that fate pushed him to meet Fallon O’ Neil.<br /><br />Fallon and Ben meet on her last day in L.A., before she moves to New York City. Ben’s unexpected, easygoing and entirely charming demeanor unnerves Fallon… in the best possible way.<br /><br />For Fallon, he turns a day marred with frustration and bad memories to a day marked by laughter and surprises.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“When I woke up this morning, I thought today was going to be one of the toughest days I’ve had in two years. Who knew the anniversary of the worst day of my life might possibly end on a good note.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />For Ben, he begins to fall for a girl who hides behind the cards she’s been dealt, but whose feistiness, verve and beauty, win him over all the same. Fallon becomes the muse he’s been hoping for, and a story begins to write itself with each moment they experience.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“You can’t leave yet. I’m not finished falling in love with you.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Before the day is over, they’re not ready to say goodbye. So they agree to meet once a year, for five years, on November 9th. No contact whatsoever… leaving destiny to play out as it will.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>"November 9th or nothing.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />They come together and come apart each year as circumstances change. Their story arcs and morphs into a once-in-a-lifetime romance, but not before plot twists threaten everything they’ve held on to so dearly.<br /><br /><b>
  <blockquote>“When you find love, you take it. You grab it with both hands and you do everything in your power not to let it go. You can’t just walk away from it and expect it to linger until you’re ready for it.”</blockquote>
</b><br /><br />Ben and Fallon’s story is irresistible—I couldn’t help but fall in love with them from the very beginning. Their chemistry leaps of the page with humor, passion and an endearing realness. Moreover, Hoover enlivens the story with her intangible magic where every moment feels larger than life, meaningful, and somehow entirely novel in its approach. With November 9, she once again proves that New Adult remains in the game with fresh and exciting stories impossible to forget. I dare you not to fall in love with Ben and Fallon.<br /><br />✦ ✦ ✦ ✦<br /><br /><b> Follow Vilma's Book Blog: </b> <a href="http://vilmasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Website</a> | <a href="www.facebook.com/vilmasbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/vilmasbookblog" rel="nofollow noopener"> Twitter </a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11730315223837435501" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1498640935" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1498640935" />
    <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli"><img alt="Pearl Angeli" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588420465p2/31514572.jpg" /></a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1498640935?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pearl Angeli" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pearl Angeli" href="/user/show/31514572-pearl-angeli">Pearl Angeli</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=fangirling">fangirling</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=sobfest">sobfest</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=highly-recommended-na">highly-recommended-na</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=i-laughed-hard">i-laughed-hard</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=2016-reads">2016-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=cute-book-couple">cute-book-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=new-adult-contemporary">new-adult-contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=mind-blown">mind-blown</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31514572-pearl-angeli?shelf=owned-physical-copy">owned-physical-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1498640935" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17486886702656380231"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You left with my soul in your fists and my heart in your teeth, and I don’t want either of them back." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Colleen Hoover, what did you just do to my heart? You just turned me into a crying mess! Now I'm in a full on sob fest.<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452671228ra/17723620.gif' width='300' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I don't think this review of mine can give justice to this amazing novel but let me just tell you that <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25111004.November_9' title='November 9 by Colleen Hoover' rel='nofollow noopener'>November 9</a> is simply beautiful! And beautiful does not even begin to describe it. It's <b>BOOK-WORTHY</b>. The kind of book that will hook you, consume you, and OWN you</span>
  <span id="freeText17486886702656380231" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You left with my soul in your fists and my heart in your teeth, and I don’t want either of them back." </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Colleen Hoover, what did you just do to my heart? You just turned me into a crying mess! Now I'm in a full on sob fest.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452671228ra/17723620.gif" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't think this review of mine can give justice to this amazing novel but let me just tell you that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25111004.November_9" title="November 9 by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">November 9</a> is simply beautiful! And beautiful does not even begin to describe it. It's <b>BOOK-WORTHY</b>. The kind of book that will hook you, consume you, and OWN you from the very beginning up to end.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25111004.November_9" title="November 9 by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">November 9</a> begins when <b>Fallon O'Neil</b> and <b>Ben Kessler</b> met at a restaurant in Los Angeles on the 9th of November. Despite having an instant connection with each other, Fallon thought that she's not yet ready to fall in love and commit herself into a relationship, thus she told Ben that she'll start dating him only when she reach the age of 23-- which will be five years after their first meeting. Before she moved to New York, they both decided to meet once a year-- same place, same date-- November 9. <br><br>So I thought that was just all about it. And I was wrong. Because there were too many things that happened in this book and the PLOT was done in an outrageous and intricate manner. That's how I know that Colleen Hoover once again did a great job-- when she was able to make me pause and contemplate about the series of events in the story. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"When you find love, you take it. You grab it with both hands and you do everything in your power not to let it go. You can’t just walk away from it and expect it to linger until you’re ready for it.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>What especially made me love the book were the main characters. Ben and Fallon are well fleshed-out characters. Ben especially. This man. I appreciate Ben's character because it's so easy to connect with him. He has a way words that can melt one's heart. Not to mention what a damn hot writer he is. And Fallon-- although I had some issues with her inconsistency, I grew to love her as I began to see how she became a fairly strong and well-developed character from being weak. And well, she's a book lover and that makes her still a likeable character.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"One of the things I always try to remind myself is that everyone has scars. A lot of them even worse than mine. The only difference is that mine are visible and most people’s aren’t."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>The <b>romance</b> is one of the book's greatest strengths. Ben and Fallon's story was poignant and heart-wrenching. All throughout the story I found myself getting scared as to what was going to happen. I got so into the book and I became really nervous because anything could happen. And wow, just when you think it can’t get anymore emotional or heartbreaking, the greatest <b>PLOT TWIST OF ALL PLOT TWISTS</b> happened and then that's it. I was destroyed. My heart was shattered into a million different pieces. You did it all over again, Colleen Hoover!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>It took four years for me to fall in love with him. It only took four pages to stop.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Colleen Hoover's writing style once again dumbfounded me. It never really gets old to be honest. But I guess I appreciate her more in this book. Her writing here separates <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25111004.November_9" title="November 9 by Colleen Hoover" rel="nofollow noopener">November 9</a> from all the contemporary books I've read and even from her previous books, because the concept is unique and amazing. The whole premise and the story itself completely stole my heart, made me smile, fall in love, drown in tears, and reflect the messages behind. <b>I LOVE NOVEMBER 9!</b> Simply one of a kind. It's now a new favorite of mine-- one I will never forget for a very long time!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>She’s not the kind of girl you choose your battles for. She’s the kind of girl you fight to the death for.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br> <b>P.S.</b> Listen to "High Hopes" by Kodaline when you read this book. The feels! <br><br>Rating:<br><br>More than<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993136i/16730745.jpg" width="200" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><p>
  <a href="https://bibliopearl.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446199662i/16763926._SX540_.jpg" alt="Pearl's Book Journey (1)" width="380" height="190" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445993261i/16730770.jpg" width="200" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_3636629324" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3636629324" />
    <a title="Giorgia ~ Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/97546350-giorgia-reads"><img alt="Giorgia ~ Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597878668p2/97546350.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3636629324?book_show_action=true">Nov 09, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giorgia ~ Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giorgia ~ Reads" href="/user/show/97546350-giorgia-reads">Giorgia ~ Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=dramatic-angsty-romance">dramatic-angsty-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=2020-read">2020-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/97546350-giorgia-reads?shelf=skimmed">skimmed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3636629324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3015657095250653000"><b> 2 stars</b> <br/><br/>I hated this book but I’m too lazy to tell you why so I’m gonna make it brief. <br/><br/>I’ve finished several books over the past couple of weeks but I’m going through a phase where I can’t express myself<i> (more like I’m too lazy to articulate anything)</i> so the reviews will have to wait. <br/><br/>I seem to be in the minority of people who did not enjoy this, so if you did, don’t read this, I’m not being nice. <br/><br/>All I’m gonna say is that this didn’t have just one thing wrong with it, but several. The 2 stars </span>
  <span id="freeText3015657095250653000" style="display:none"><b> 2 stars</b> <br /><br />I hated this book but I’m too lazy to tell you why so I’m gonna make it brief. <br /><br />I’ve finished several books over the past couple of weeks but I’m going through a phase where I can’t express myself<i> (more like I’m too lazy to articulate anything)</i> so the reviews will have to wait. <br /><br />I seem to be in the minority of people who did not enjoy this, so if you did, don’t read this, I’m not being nice. <br /><br />All I’m gonna say is that this didn’t have just one thing wrong with it, but several. The 2 stars are for the writing, which is good and consistent.<br /><br />The plot - I wasn’t a fan of. I usually dislike it when flimsy excuses are used for a couple to not be together. I DIDN’T buy it! I mean, come on, that was a lazy plot device and not believable. The whole “we’ll meet every year on Nov 9th only, and not talk the rest of the time”.. huh 🤔 call me crazy but there’s other options?! Again, call me completely cuckoo, but if you’re so attracted, semi in love with someone that’s not a normal go-to reaction. And how do you go about dating and being with others if you’re waiting for the next nov. 9th to spend it with the person you supposedly “love”. That’s wrong and unfair. I mean, come on, what a load of c**p. And the thing is that, it’s so obvious that the whole scenario I just talked about was written that way to make the book “unique”, “interesting”, “mysterious”, “original” blah blah BLAH. Without that whole concept there would be no book really. <br /><br />I hated Ben. I’m not in the mood to list all the reasons why, but he was just icky. As for Fallon, she was just so insecure and meh. I get insecurity, but I also learned of a concept called growth and confidence so sue me, but I’d love to read about the latter two. <br /><br />And now the <b>BIGGEST</b> no-no, everybody, I give you :<b> the twist</b>. No, just no. Jesus H. Christ no! It tainted everything for me. I already wasn’t particularly enamoured with this book and I had a pretty good idea this was gonna be the twist, but I thought the explanation was gonna be different but NO, it was horrible. Ben is straight up sick in the head! And everything that happened in this book, I started seeing it through a very different perspective and let me tell you, there’s nothing romantic about it. (Also, who leaves that kind of note?! Like that’s just straight up bad writing cause I just don’t think it’s realistic - if you read it you know what I’m taking about) <br /><br />There’s loads to say but I just wanted to quickly cover this before I lose my steam cause the story is very fresh in my head atm. <br /><br />If you wanna know all the messed up details before going into it, read the 1/2 star reviews, they are right!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3015657095250653000" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1147995719?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hulya Kara Yuksel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hulya Kara Yuksel" href="/user/show/32793174-hulya-kara-yuksel">Hulya Kara Yuksel</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25092686-november-9">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1147995719" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16123664690746018296"><b>
  <i>“When you find love, you take it. You grab it with both hands and you do everything in your power not to let it go. You can’t just walk away from it and expect it to linger until you’re ready for it.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>I remember just like it was yesterday…. Almost 1 year ago when I was first add this book to my TBR shelf I was pretty excited. Because Colleen is my all time favorite author and anything she writes can’t never disappoint me. Yeah, I’m so sure of that and she proved to me that I’m not wrong about</span>
  <span id="freeText16123664690746018296" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“When you find love, you take it. You grab it with both hands and you do everything in your power not to let it go. You can’t just walk away from it and expect it to linger until you’re ready for it.”</i>
</b><br><br>I remember just like it was yesterday…. Almost 1 year ago when I was first add this book to my TBR shelf I was pretty excited. Because Colleen is my all time favorite author and anything she writes can’t never disappoint me. Yeah, I’m so sure of that and she proved to me that I’m not wrong about her. And she did it again. She stole my heart once again with one of hers fictional boys…<br><br>As I said, I was waitin this book for months and when the time hit midnight and as soon as this book showed on my e-reader I started to read it. And almost right after 1st chapter -yeah that amazing 1st chapter- I was captivated by the story. I already gave myself to the book and I just couldn’t stop reading Ben &amp; Fallon’s story. Their chemistry was perfect. I loved them so much. I just loved every single word, every good / happy / sad / bad moment in this book. And right now I'm not capable to write the summary of the book for you so pls forgive me for that and I don't want to give you spoilers etc so you just have to read this book. And I hope you feel / live those moments just like me while you're readin it.! :)<br><br>Colleen, my Queen. You make me feel alive whenever I read one of yours books. You’re making me feel this characters happines and sadness. It’s like I’m living that moment with them. Literally. That’s why I love you so much. Once again thank you so much for your beautiful words and God bless you… :)<br><br>Oh by the way, I have to confess one thing. Whenever I start a new CoHo book I exactly know how am gonna feel it while I’ m reading the book. First I’ll laugh, then I'll laugh a lot, then a couple tears will drops on my cheeks and then more laughs and then more tears, too much tears, I cannot stop that damn tears!!! And then booom! I’m crying like a river. This woman always does this thing to me. But I’ll forgive her for making me cry because this book (or the other books of hers) deserves every single of my tears. They're all beautiful. So fucking beautiful…<br><br>PS. I’ll share some quotes from this book or maybe a lot of quotes. Because I have a lot of favorite moments on this book. (For example: When they were at the airport. Slow Mo scene was perfect...):) So if you’re wanna read them first just before you start to read the book go ahead it's your desicion but <b>please give this book a chance to change your life. Trust me, you won’t regret it. </b><br><br><b>I read this book with my sweet and gorgeous friend Ana. Maybe she didn't cry too much just like I did but she definitely got emotional a lot. :D<br><br>I'll see you on our next BR honey.<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/13346584-ana">https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/1...</a></b><br><br>----------------------<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418490792ra/12810366.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1415567708ra/11812782.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443141301ra/16323138.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>----------------------<br><br>“If we’re going to kiss, it has to be book-worthy.”<br><br>“All I care about is you. Being with you every day. Seeing you every day. I’m not finished falling in love with you yet.”<br><br>“It’s easy to fall in love, Ben. The hard part comes when you want out.”<br><br>”His hand squeezes my waist and he eyes me hard. “Fallon.” He says my name like it’s an entire lecture in itself.”<br><br>“I wrap my arms around her and pull her against me and when I feel her arms go around me, I do the most non-alpha thing I can possibly do. I cry like a fucking baby.”<br><br>“You left with my soul in your fists and my heart in your teeth, and I don’t want either of them back.”<br><br>“When you find love, you take it. You grab it with both hands and you do everything in your power not to let it go. You can’t just walk away from it and expect it to linger until you’re ready for it.”<br><br>“If she’s not careful, I might just fall in love with her. Tonight.”<br><br>“Another tear falls, but this time it falls from my eye. I take a step back and I let go of her.”<br><br>“So whether or not you can find it in your heart to love me again, I needed to thank you for saving me. And if there is any part of you capable of forgiving me, you know where I’ll be. Tonight, next year, the next, for eternity. The choice is yours.”<br><br>“All I want is for you to be happy. That’s all I’ve ever wanted. And I’ll do anything to make that happen for you, even if it means helping you to forget me.”<br><br>“I don’t want to be your first, Fallon. I want to be your last.”<br><br>“He presses his mouth to mine and kisses me with so much emotion, I forget all the things. Everything. I forget where I am. Who I am.”<br><br>“If you don’t show up today, I’ll be there next year. And the next. Every November 9th I’ll wait for you, hoping one day you’ll be able to find enough forgiveness to love me again. But if that doesn’t happen and you never show, I’ll still be grateful to you until the day that I die. You saved me the day we met.”<br><br>“I’ve never needed to wrap my arms around someone more than I do right now, and I’d give anything to have her here with me. To just be able to press my face in her hair and feel her arms around my waist, her hands on my back. There isn’t a single thing in this world that could comfort me like she could, but I didn’t tell her that. I couldn’t.”<br><br>“Don't stop" I tease in a seductive voice. " Give me more, Ben. Did you read eBooks or..." I run my finger slowly down his chest."Hardbacks?"<br>He pulls his hands behind his head and a smug look washes over his face. "Oh, they were hardbacks, all right. And I'm not sure if you're ready for this, but...I have my own TBR pile. You should read it, Fallon. It's huge"”<br><br>“I need you to know that it was always you who had my heart. And I would have never let anyone else borrow it if I knew there was a chance in hell you’d ever want it back.”<br> “But the only thing that makes me sad—the biggest thing—is that I think about you every second of every day and I don’t know how to get over you.” “Don’t,” I beg her. “Please don’t get over me.”<br><br>“You’re beautiful. Every inch of you is so beautiful.” <br><br>“And I’m in love with her. Like, really in love with her. Crippling, debilitating, paralyzing love. So please accept my sincerest apologies, because she’s coming home with me tonight. I hope. I pray.”<br><br>“I’m not sure if sex is supposed to make you feel like you’ve just lost a part of yourself to the person inside you, but that’s exactly what it felt like. It felt as if the second we joined together, a tiny piece of our souls got confused and a piece of his fell into me and a piece of mine fell into him. It was by far the single most intense moment I’ve ever shared with another person.”<br><br>“He hasn’t spoken a single word to me yet, but his actions have said a million thank yous.”<br><br>"When you left last year, you left with my soul in your hands and my heart in your teeth, and I knew I would never get either of them back. You can keep them, I don’t really need them anymore."<br><br>“You were just thinking dirty thoughts.”<br>“Was not,” I quip.<br>“Fallon, we’ve been dating for two hours now. I can read you like a book,and right now I do believe that book is full of erotica.”<br><br>“Fallon,” he whispers, moving his lips slowly across mine. “Thank you for this beautiful gift.” As soon as his words brush over my mouth, he covers me in a deep kiss. My whole body tenses from the burst of pain that ripples through me as he pushes inside of me, but the perfection of the way we fit together makes the pain a mere inconvenience. It’s beautiful. He’s beautiful. And somehow, with the way he’s looking down at me, I even believe I’m beautiful. He presses his mouth against my ear and whispers, “No combination of written words could ever do this moment justice.”</span>

<div id="review_860498447" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/860498447" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/860498447?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25092686-november-9">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer860498447" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4070544593123815890"><b>4 <i>”It’s November 9th or nothing.”</i>STARS</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>I can always count on Colleen Hoover to deliver a story that is impossible to put down. <i>November Nine</i> is no exception, this story will surely take a reader through a tough mutter of emotions. <br/><br/>Fallon and Ben’s meeting comes at such a turning point in Fallon’s life. Both characters are eighteen years of age and young Fallon is on her way to New York to pursue a career on Broadway. The two connect on so many levels that it’s impossible not to get g</span>
  <span id="freeText4070544593123815890" style="display:none"><b>4 <i>”It’s November 9th or nothing.”</i>STARS</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>I can always count on Colleen Hoover to deliver a story that is impossible to put down. <i>November Nine</i> is no exception, this story will surely take a reader through a tough mutter of emotions. <br><br>Fallon and Ben’s meeting comes at such a turning point in Fallon’s life. Both characters are eighteen years of age and young Fallon is on her way to New York to pursue a career on Broadway. The two connect on so many levels that it’s impossible not to get giddy right along with them. The two make a pact of sorts, promising to meet for the next five years on November 9th. <br><br><b>
  <i>”We’ll both get to experience like like we’re supposed to at this age, but we also get to be with each other once a year. It’s the best of both worlds.”</i>
</b><br><br>Each year, they find their way to one another while the other 365 days in between do bring changes in both their lives. Ben’s adoration and attraction for Fallon develops so much confidence for a girl who had lost so much. I just loved how Fallon blossomed throughout the story. <br><br>The couple’s interactions and dialogue was spot on, witty, tender and at times, oh so swoon worthy. <br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Going back to my tough mutter scenario, things aren't smooth sailing and Colleen Hoover goes for several crushing and WTH moments.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492029252ra/22475202.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As always, I loved the flawless beauty in the writing, as well as the characters connections, and just like <i>Confess,</i> this book didn’t need the drama or reveals for me or readers on a whole, to have slapped a 5-Star Favorite on either book. Sadly the reveal in this book only lessened the couple in my eyes. I guess what I’m trying to say is that Colleen Hoover’s writing stands on its own and she doesn’t need to shock me because she <b>ALWAYS</b> has me from the first few chapters. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447188500ra/16967284.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4070544593123815890" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_892150199" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/892150199" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/892150199?book_show_action=true">Mar 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer892150199" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7528004897316472608"><b>4-4.5 Stars!!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447341358i/16989911.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Once again Colleen Hoover delivered a unique story that will stay with me for a while. This book like some others I have read from her, it made feel, really FEEL. It made me smile, it made me shed a tear or two and it made me care, really care for these two endearing characters. <i>“November 9”</i> was original from start to finish, it was beautifully written, with a fantastically executed plot and a love story that melt my heart.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I thought I was stronger than a word, but I just di</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7528004897316472608" style="display:none"><b>4-4.5 Stars!!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447341358i/16989911.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once again Colleen Hoover delivered a unique story that will stay with me for a while. This book like some others I have read from her, it made feel, really FEEL. It made me smile, it made me shed a tear or two and it made me care, really care for these two endearing characters. <i>“November 9”</i> was original from start to finish, it was beautifully written, with a fantastically executed plot and a love story that melt my heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I thought I was stronger than a word, but I just discovered that having to say goodbye to you is by far the hardest thing I’ve ever had to do.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>November 9 is not just a simply date for Fallon O’Neill. Is the day her life changed irrevocably, is the day that changed her forever, is the day she would give anything to forget. But is also the date when she met Benton James Kessler. Ben is a college student, an aspiring novelist, a boy for whom November 9 has a certain significance. From the moment he meets Fallon, he is drawn to her and not only to her beauty, but to her personality as well. He sees the real Fallon, he doesn’t see the scarred, insecure girl who tried to hide from the world. And Fallon is drawn to Ben as well. They connect with each other from the start and they agree to spend this day, November 9 with each other. Despite the strong connection between them, they part ways, Fallon moving to New York to pursue a career on Broadway, but they agree to meet on the same day at the same place for the next five years. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447341358i/16989912.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“November 9”</i> is that kind of a book you need to experience for yourself, so I’m not going to give anything else away. Like I mentioned above this fantastic tale was original from start to finish. I loved the concept of the story. It was intriguing, unique and of course every chapter left me wanting more. <br><br>I absolutely loved this beautiful, unconventional love story between these two characters. Their love story made my heart ache, but they also made it melt. It was simply wonderful, believable and beautifully told. Colleen’s flawless, poetic writing made me devour this story. I lived it, I felt it, I fall in love with it. <br><br>I loved these two characters. Both Fallon and Ben were flawed characters, very well portrayed in such a great way. They were endearing, have depth and they were relatable. Fallon was an easy character to like from the start. At first she was portrayed as a vulnerable young girl, but as the story progressed we get to know a different Fallon – much stronger and more confident and I have to say I loved the ‘new Fallon’. I sympathize so much with her, but I’m not gonna lie, there were times when I really wanted to slap her. Needless to say I didn’t agree with all her actions. <br><br>Ben was a wonderful character and I fell in love with him from the very beginning. He was sweet and thoughtful, attentive and considerate, but what I loved the most about him was the way he made Fallon feels about herself. For Fallon he was like a breath of fresh air. I loved the way he talked with her, his gestures, his flirting, his sweet, sweet words.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1447341358i/16989913.jpg" width="400" height="465" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I adored their magical connection. You know why? Because I felt it with every fiber of my being. It was palpable from the beginning and I truly loved it. Fallon and Ben were wonderful together and their relationship warmed my heart. They completed each other in every single way and at times I really believed they were soul mates. <br><br>The story flowed fantastically well and the time jumps never felt too much. At times it was intense, angsty, but I loved every minute of it. What I didn’t like too much was the drama – unnecessary drama I could say. It was too much IMO.<br><br>Overall, a wonderful read!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This is real life, and in the real world you have to bust your ass for the happy ever after… When you find love, you take it. You grab it with both hands and you do everything in your power not to let it go. You can’t just walk away from it and expect it to linger until you’re ready for it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="7528004897316472608" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7159797802786209931"> <b>4 STARS<br/><br/>“You’ll never be able to find yourself if you’re lost in someone else.” <br/></b><br/><br/>What I love about Colleen Hoover is that her stories are always unique and brilliant! This book is not an exception, it’s simply amazing, heartwarming, sweet, funny and intense. The writing is so poetic and addictive that once you start reading the book you can't put it down until you finish it!<br/><br/>I start it yesterday and I read it so fast because I wanted to know what was going to happen to Fallon and Ben! This story t</span>
  <span id="freeText7159797802786209931" style="display:none"> <b>4 STARS<br><br>“You’ll never be able to find yourself if you’re lost in someone else.” <br></b><br><br>What I love about Colleen Hoover is that her stories are always unique and brilliant! This book is not an exception, it’s simply amazing, heartwarming, sweet, funny and intense. The writing is so poetic and addictive that once you start reading the book you can't put it down until you finish it!<br><br>I start it yesterday and I read it so fast because I wanted to know what was going to happen to Fallon and Ben! This story touched me so much, I couldn't stop crying feeling everything Fallon and Ben were going through! I will not say anything about the plot because it's so unique and I think whatever I say will break the magic of reading it. But be prepared for an emotional story with some twists that leave you anxious to see what will happen! <br><br>Ben and Fallon are the most adorable and cute couple I have ever read!!They are so sweet, funny and lovable characters that you can't stop yourself from falling in love with them and their story! Their connection is evident from the start and you can see that something magical will happen between them! Fallon is insecure and vulnerable due to her scars and Ben is the one who will help her feel good with herself. Ben has his own issues, and that’s a mystery for us, one that is revealed during the progression of their story. <br><br><b>“I’m not finished falling in love with you yet.”</b><br><br> I’m giving it only 4 stars even though I said so many things about how much I loved it!!There are a specific moment in the book that I was upset with Ben. I can understand why he did what he did but I can't forget about it and it bothered me. Overall it was a beautiful story that you should everybody read it!!Colleen Hoover as always did an amazing job!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1408634948ra/10876724.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> </span>

The author uses and combines words in such a beautiful way as if to create harmony. She always uses less to achieve more. Her messages are simple yet so complex and true.   <span id="freeText16178768893590198961" style="display:none"><b>I hated this book.</b> I wanted to rate it one star last night. I was so angry. But apparently the morning is smarter than the evening. I am still pissed. The first twist in the book is stupid and unnecessary.<br><br><b>I loved this book.</b> The story is amazing. The writing is amazing. The author uses and combines words in such a beautiful way as if to create harmony. She always uses less to achieve more. Her messages are simple yet so complex and true. Her characters are simply beautiful, inside and out, flaws and all. She describes them in such an amazing way that even their flaws seem perfect.
